   163â†’    fn eval_expr(&mut self, expr: &Expr) -> DslResult<Value> {
   164â†’        match &expr.node {
   165â†’            ExprKind::Literal(lit) => Ok(Value::from(lit)),
   166â†’
   167â†’            ExprKind::Ident(name) => self.eval_ident(name, expr.span),
   168â†’
   169â†’            ExprKind::List(items) => {
   170â†’                let values: DslResult<Vec<_>> = items.iter().map(|e| self.eval_expr(e)).collect();
   171â†’                Ok(Value::List(values?))
   172â†’            }
   173â†’
   174â†’            ExprKind::Call(call) => self.eval_call(call, None, expr.span),
   175â†’
   176â†’            ExprKind::Pipe(left, call) => {
   177â†’                // Evaluate the left side first
   178â†’                let left_value = self.eval_expr(left)?;
   179â†’                // Then evaluate the call with the piped value
   180â†’                self.eval_call(call, Some(left_value), expr.span)
   181â†’            }
   182â†’
   183â†’            ExprKind::Paren(inner) => self.eval_expr(inner),
   184â†’        }
   185â†’    }
   186â†’
   187â†’    /// Evaluate an identifier reference.
   188â†’    fn eval_ident(&self, name: &str, span: Span) -> DslResult<Value> {
   189â†’        // Check variables first
   190â†’        if let Some(value) = self.variables.get(name) {
   191â†’            return Ok(value.clone());
   192â†’        }
   193â†’
   194â†’        // Check if it's a known slot name - return a reference
   195â†’        if let Ok(_slot) = parse_slot_name(name) {
   196â†’            return Ok(Value::SlotRef(name.to_string()));
   197â†’        }
   198â†’
   199â†’        // Unknown identifier
   200â†’        Err(DslError::new(
   201â†’            DslErrorKind::Parse(format!("Unknown identifier '{}'", name)),
   202â†’            span,
   203â†’        ))
   204â†’    }
   205â†’

   213â†’        })?;
   214â†’

   219â†’        // Process positional arguments

   228â†’                            params.insert(param_def.name.to_string(), param_value);
   229â†’                        }
   230â†’                    }
   231â†’                    positional_index += 1;
   232â†’                }
   233â†’                Arg::Named { name, value } => {
   234â†’                    let val = self.eval_expr(value)?;
   235â†’                    if let Some(param_value) = val.to_param_value() {
   236â†’                        params.insert(name.clone(), param_value);
   237â†’                    }
   238â†’                }
   239â†’            }
   240â†’        }
   241â†’
   242â†’        // Set parameters on context
   243â†’        for (key, value) in params {
   244â†’            self.context.set_param(&key, value);
   245â†’        }
   246â†’
   247â†’        // Execute the primitive
   248â†’        primitive
   249â†’            .execute(&mut self.context)

# Phase 5: Complete Incremental Execution

## Summary

Enable the DSL evaluator to skip cached prefix steps and only execute the uncached suffix, significantly speeding up iterative analysis.

## Current State

**What works:**
- `find_longest_cached_prefix()` correctly identifies cached steps
- `steps_cached` is reported in response
- Output files are saved to disk after each evaluation
- `load_session_data_for_eval_with_tracking()` loads ALL data files at start

**What's missing:**
- The evaluator still executes the ENTIRE pipeline (TODO at line 769)
- Cached prefix outputs exist on disk but we re-compute them anyway

## Key Insight

The cached prefix's output data **is already loaded** at eval start:
```
Expression: counts |> filter() |> tmm() |> pca()
                                    â†‘
                              Cached prefix ends here
                              (filtered_counts.csv, normalized_counts.csv already on disk)

At eval start: load_session_data_for_eval_with_tracking() loads:
  - counts.csv â†’ context.Counts
  - filtered_counts.csv â†’ context.FilteredCounts
  - normalized_counts.csv â†’ context.NormalizedCounts  â† Cached output!

We just need to skip steps 0-2 and only run step 3 (pca).
```

## Implementation Approach

### Option A: Build suffix expression and evaluate it â­ CHOSEN

Build a new AST where the source is a reference to the cached output slot, then pipe to remaining calls.

**Example:**
```
Original: counts |> filter(0.1) |> tmm() |> pca()
Cached prefix: counts |> filter(0.1) |> tmm() (step index 2)

Built suffix: normalized_counts |> pca()
             â†‘ This slot name is the output of tmm()
```

**Why this approach:**
- Clean separation - evaluator unchanged
- Uses existing eval() infrastructure
- Easy to test and debug
- Output slot name can be inferred from primitive name

### How to map primitive â†’ output slot

Create a simple mapping function:
```rust
fn primitive_output_slot(primitive_name: &str) -> Option<&'static str> {
    match primitive_name {
        "filter_prevalence" | "filter_abundance" | "filter_variance" => Some("filtered_counts"),
        "tmm" | "median_of_ratios" | "upper_quartile" => Some("normalized_counts"),
        "clr" | "vst" | "rlog" | "log" | "zscore" => Some("transformed_counts"),
        "beta_diversity" => Some("distance_matrix"),
        "alpha_diversity" => Some("alpha_diversity"),
        "pca" | "pcoa" | "nmds" => Some("ordination"),
        "permanova" | "anosim" | "wald" | "lrt" => Some("p_values"),
        _ => None,
    }
}
```

## Implementation Steps

### Step 1: Add `primitive_output_slot()` function

**File:** `bioengine/src/daemon/http.rs` (or new module)

Add the mapping function that maps primitive names to their output slot names.

### Step 2: Add `build_suffix_expr()` function

**File:** `bioforge/src/dsl/pipeline.rs`

```rust
/// Build a suffix expression from remaining pipeline steps.
///
/// Creates an expression that starts with a slot reference (the cached output)
/// and pipes through the remaining uncached steps.
pub fn build_suffix_expr(
    steps: &[PipelineStep<'_>],
    start_index: usize,
    source_slot: &str,
) -> Option<Expr> {
    if start_index >= steps.len() {
        return None;
    }

    // Start with reference to cached output
    let mut expr = Expr::new(
        ExprKind::Ident(source_slot.to_string()),
        Span::default(),
    );

    // Pipe through remaining steps
    for step in &steps[start_index..] {
        if let PipelineStep::Call { call, span } = step {
            expr = Expr::new(
                ExprKind::Pipe(Box::new(expr), (*call).clone()),
                *span,
            );
        }
    }

    Some(expr)
}
```

### Step 3: Modify eval_handler to use incremental execution

**File:** `bioengine/src/daemon/http.rs` (around line 768-785)

Replace the TODO section:

```rust
// Check for longest cached prefix
let cached_prefix = { ... };  // existing code

let (result, steps_executed) = if let Some((cached_idx, _, _)) = &cached_prefix {
    // Incremental execution: skip cached prefix
    let cached_step = &pipeline_steps[*cached_idx];
    let primitive_name = cached_step.name().unwrap_or("unknown");

    if let Some(output_slot) = primitive_output_slot(primitive_name) {
        // Build suffix expression starting after cached step
        let suffix_start = cached_idx + 1;

        if suffix_start < pipeline_steps.len() {
            // Build and evaluate suffix only
            if let Some(suffix_expr) = build_suffix_expr(
                &pipeline_steps,
                suffix_start,
                output_slot,
            ) {
                let result = evaluator.eval(&suffix_expr)?;
                (result, pipeline_steps.len() - suffix_start)
            } else {
                // Fallback: evaluate full expression
                (evaluator.eval(&expr)?, pipeline_steps.len())
            }
        } else {
            // Cached entire pipeline - return cached output reference
            (Value::SlotRef(output_slot.to_string()), 0)
        }
    } else {
        // Unknown primitive output - fallback to full eval
        (evaluator.eval(&expr)?, pipeline_steps.len())
    }
} else {
    // No cached prefix - evaluate full expression
    (evaluator.eval(&expr)?, pipeline_steps.len())
};
```

### Step 4: Update response to show actual execution

Update the response JSON to show `steps_executed` correctly:
```rust
"pipeline": {
    "steps_total": steps_total,
    "steps_cached": steps_cached,
    "steps_executed": steps_executed,  // Use actual count
    "incremental": steps_cached > 0 && steps_executed < steps_total,
}
```

3. Eval of `counts |> filter() |> tmm() |> pca()` executes only 1 step (pca)

| `bioengine/src/daemon/http.rs` | Add `primitive_output_slot()`, modify eval_handler |

## Success Criteria

- [ ] `counts |> filter() |> tmm()` caches correctly (existing)
- [ ] `counts |> filter() |> tmm() |> pca()` only executes `pca()` step
- [ ] Response shows `"steps_executed": 1` for incremental run
- [ ] Response shows `"incremental": true` flag
- [ ] Performance: incremental eval completes faster than full eval

## Edge Cases

1. **Unknown primitive**: Fall back to full evaluation
2. **No cached prefix**: Normal full evaluation
3. **Entire pipeline cached**: Return cached result (existing behavior)
4. **Source step only cached**: Start from step 1 (first call)

## Approved Plan:
# Phase 5: Complete Incremental Execution

## Summary

Enable the DSL evaluator to skip cached prefix steps and only execute the uncached suffix, significantly speeding up iterative analysis.

## Current State

**What works:**
- `find_longest_cached_prefix()` correctly identifies cached steps
- `steps_cached` is reported in response
- Output files are saved to disk after each evaluation
- `load_session_data_for_eval_with_tracking()` loads ALL data files at start

**What's missing:**
- The evaluator still executes the ENTIRE pipeline (TODO at line 769)
- Cached prefix outputs exist on disk but we re-compute them anyway

## Key Insight

The cached prefix's output data **is already loaded** at eval start:
```
Expression: counts |> filter() |> tmm() |> pca()
                                    â†‘
                              Cached prefix ends here
                              (filtered_counts.csv, normalized_counts.csv already on disk)

At eval start: load_session_data_for_eval_with_tracking() loads:
  - counts.csv â†’ context.Counts
  - filtered_counts.csv â†’ context.FilteredCounts
  - normalized_counts.csv â†’ context.NormalizedCounts  â† Cached output!

We just need to skip steps 0-2 and only run step 3 (pca).
```

## Implementation Approach

### Option A: Build suffix expression and evaluate it â­ CHOSEN

Build a new AST where the source is a reference to the cached output slot, then pipe to remaining calls.

**Example:**
```
Original: counts |> filter(0.1) |> tmm() |> pca()
Cached prefix: counts |> filter(0.1) |> tmm() (step index 2)

Built suffix: normalized_counts |> pca()
             â†‘ This slot name is the output of tmm()
```

**Why this approach:**
- Clean separation - evaluator unchanged
- Uses existing eval() infrastructure
- Easy to test and debug
- Output slot name can be inferred from primitive name

### How to map primitive â†’ output slot

Create a simple mapping function:
```rust
fn primitive_output_slot(primitive_name: &str) -> Option<&'static str> {
    match primitive_name {
        "filter_prevalence" | "filter_abundance" | "filter_variance" => Some("filtered_counts"),
        "tmm" | "median_of_ratios" | "upper_quartile" => Some("normalized_counts"),
        "clr" | "vst" | "rlog" | "log" | "zscore" => Some("transformed_counts"),
        "beta_diversity" => Some("distance_matrix"),
        "alpha_diversity" => Some("alpha_diversity"),
        "pca" | "pcoa" | "nmds" => Some("ordination"),
        "permanova" | "anosim" | "wald" | "lrt" => Some("p_values"),
        _ => None,
    }
}
```

---

## Implementation Steps

### Step 1: Add `primitive_output_slot()` function

**File:** `bioengine/src/daemon/http.rs` (or new module)

Add the mapping function that maps primitive names to their output slot names.

### Step 2: Add `build_suffix_expr()` function

**File:** `bioforge/src/dsl/pipeline.rs`

```rust
/// Build a suffix expression from remaining pipeline steps.
///
/// Creates an expression that starts with a slot reference (the cached output)
/// and pipes through the remaining uncached steps.
pub fn build_suffix_expr(
    steps: &[PipelineStep<'_>],
    start_index: usize,
    source_slot: &str,
) -> Option<Expr> {
    if start_index >= steps.len() {
        return None;
    }

    // Start with reference to cached output
    let mut expr = Expr::new(
        ExprKind::Ident(source_slot.to_string()),
        Span::default(),
    );

    // Pipe through remaining steps
    for step in &steps[start_index..] {
        if let PipelineStep::Call { call, span } = step {
            expr = Expr::new(
                ExprKind::Pipe(Box::new(expr), (*call).clone()),
                *span,
            );
        }
    }

    Some(expr)
}
```

### Step 3: Modify eval_handler to use incremental execution

**File:** `bioengine/src/daemon/http.rs` (around line 768-785)

Replace the TODO section:

```rust
// Check for longest cached prefix
let cached_prefix = { ... };  // existing code

let (result, steps_executed) = if let Some((cached_idx, _, _)) = &cached_prefix {
    // Incremental execution: skip cached prefix
    let cached_step = &pipeline_steps[*cached_idx];
    let primitive_name = cached_step.name().unwrap_or("unknown");

    if let Some(output_slot) = primitive_output_slot(primitive_name) {
        // Build suffix expression starting after cached step
        let suffix_start = cached_idx + 1;

        if suffix_start < pipeline_steps.len() {
            // Build and evaluate suffix only
            if let Some(suffix_expr) = build_suffix_expr(
                &pipeline_steps,
                suffix_start,
                output_slot,
            ) {
                let result = evaluator.eval(&suffix_expr)?;
                (result, pipeline_steps.len() - suffix_start)
            } else {
                // Fallback: evaluate full expression
                (evaluator.eval(&expr)?, pipeline_steps.len())
            }
        } else {
            // Cached entire pipeline - return cached output reference
            (Value::SlotRef(output_slot.to_string()), 0)
        }
    } else {
        // Unknown primitive output - fallback to full eval
        (evaluator.eval(&expr)?, pipeline_steps.len())
    }
} else {
    // No cached prefix - evaluate full expression
    (evaluator.eval(&expr)?, pipeline_steps.len())
};
```

### Step 4: Update response to show actual execution

Update the response JSON to show `steps_executed` correctly:
```rust
"pipeline": {
    "steps_total": steps_total,
    "steps_cached": steps_cached,
    "steps_executed": steps_executed,  // Use actual count
    "incremental": steps_cached > 0 && steps_executed < steps_total,
}
```

### Step 5: Add test for incremental execution

**File:** `bioengine/tests/incremental_eval_test.rs` (new)

Test that:
1. First eval of `counts |> filter() |> tmm()` executes 3 steps
2. Second eval of same expression returns cached (0 steps)
3. Eval of `counts |> filter() |> tmm() |> pca()` executes only 1 step (pca)

---

## Files to Modify

| File | Changes |
|------|---------|
| `bioforge/src/dsl/pipeline.rs` | Add `build_suffix_expr()` |
| `bioengine/src/daemon/http.rs` | Add `primitive_output_slot()`, modify eval_handler |

## Success Criteria

- [ ] `counts |> filter() |> tmm()` caches correctly (existing)
- [ ] `counts |> filter() |> tmm() |> pca()` only executes `pca()` step
- [ ] Response shows `"steps_executed": 1` for incremental run
- [ ] Response shows `"incremental": true` flag
- [ ] Performance: incremental eval completes faster than full eval

## Edge Cases

1. **Unknown primitive**: Fall back to full evaluation
2. **No cached prefix**: Normal full evaluation
3. **Entire pipeline cached**: Return cached result (existing behavior)
4. **Source step only cached**: Start from step 1 (first call)
